posted:Posted February 27, 2024
msg:Jenny at the front desk upgraded the room type for free, from premium to sea view, and called half a day in advance to inquire about the arrival time and situation. She helped to renew the room the next day, which was very good.

Highlights: The facilities in the room are first-class. It is warm as if there is a fresh air system when you enter the door facing south. The hotel is newly renovated as a whole. It is a modern light luxury style that has been popular in the past two years. The materials are solid. The parking lot in the basement is spacious and the lobby is magnificent. The cleaning sister is very polite and moves quickly. The heated swimming pool and gym are clean. Special reminder: The snacks and pork shop for afternoon tea are delicious. Breakfast is delivered to the room at the scheduled time. It is very 5-star üëçüèªüëçüèª There is Chinese food on the second floor of the hotel, which can be ordered and the environment is good.

Points that can be improved
You can bring a towel to the swimming pool. Although it is open to the public, there is no one, which is very inconvenient. The management of the personnel on the second floor should be strengthened. It is very chaotic. There are all kinds of noises lying on the sofa while playing with mobile phones.

There will be engine sounds when fishing boats go out to sea in the early morning in the sea view room. Jenny kindly reminded that earplugs are also provided, but I personally think it is okay. It depends on the person.

There are no particularly outstanding sights or food around the hotel, and even having a cup of coffee is difficult, but the hotel environment is indeed good and suitable for relaxation.
